class=\"shopify-section\"><section data-section-id=\"1484237681559\">\n  \n  <div class=\"section-title row\">\n    <h2>Why Shop Authentic Discount Watches at DWS?</h2>\n  </div>\n  \n  <p></p><p>When asked this question, most websites will likely try to explain that they have an extensive selection of products on sale at great price points, as well as great service. This may be true, but if everybody is indeed claiming the same thing; then really, why should I shop with you?</p><p>\n\n</p><p>At Discount Watch Store, we have all of those too – the extensive selection of discount watches, and the <b>cheapest prices</b> you can find, not to mention <b>quality service</b>. We have an extensive selection of watches from <b>over 50 name brands like Bulova, Casio, Citizen, <a href=\"/collections/fossil-watches\">Fossil</a>, <a href=\"/collections/invicta-watches\">Invicta</a>, <a href=\"/collections/michael-kors-watches\">Michael Kors</a>, Nixon, Seiko, Tissot</b> and so much more. We regularly monitor our competitors’ pricing and adjust our own to remain competitive. Often times, we lead the way and our competitors have no choice but to follow suit.</p>\n\n<p>We have real people answering phone calls, but we believe what really sets us apart is that we take the time to make sure that the item on sale is in perfect, mint condition. While manufacturers, and other retailers may have a quality control protocol that involves spot checks on a mere 2% to 5% of their products, <b>we check nearly every single watch we sell twice</b>. This includes once before it goes on our shelves and once before we ship it. It takes us literally hundreds of hours each month to accomplish this highly labor intensive task.</p>\n\n<p>Why do we bother with this outwardly tedious process when the actual overall defect rates across all watch brands we carry are less than 2% to begin with? Well, that's because 2% is just not acceptable to us. In the real world, 2% means 2 customers out of every 100 will receive defective pieces on average. Would you like it if you were one of those 2 customers? I am sure the answer will be a resounding no.</p>\n<p>\nWith our rigorous QC process, <b>our product defect rate is less than 0.05%</b>. So for every 10,000 orders we have less than 5 watches that have some sort of product defect, and that's including any damages resulted from shipping carriers mishandling the packages. This makes Discount Watch Store the best place to buy watches.</p>\n\n<p>On top of all this, we also have a <b>90 day money back guarantee</b>, and a <b>best price guarantee</b> for our already discounted watches, ensuring the cheapest prices anywhere on the web.</p>\n<p>\nSo we return to the initial question: why should I shop with you? The answer is simple: you should buy watches online from Discount Watch Store because WE CARE.</p><p></p>\n</section>\n\n<style>\n  p {\n  \tfont-size: 12pt !important;\n    padding: 0 10%;\n
